Passive Empress's Shout
Master Level 1
Description Permanently increases Max HP and Max MP.
Level 1 Max HP and Max MP: +20%


Active Empress's Prayer
Master Level 1
Description [Master Level: 1]
Increase Attack Power and Magic ATT, allowing you to attack higher-level monsters. The effect remains active even if you are KO'd. Does not stack with Hero's Echo. While Empress's Prayer is active, you cannot receive the effects of Hero's Echo.
Cooldown: 1 day
Not affected by cooldown reset or buff duration increase.
Level 1 MP Cost: 30, Attack Power and Magic ATT: +4%
Show/hide all levels
Active Knight's Watch
Master Level 3
Description Knight's Watch blocks damage from enemies and increases your damage for a set time. Increases Status Resistance for a short time when used as a Link Skill.
Level 1 Barrier Duration: 15 sec, Enemy Blows Blocked: 3, Damage: +15%
Damage -10% only for attacks that inflict damage at a certain ratio of the Max HP
Cooldown: 180 sec
3 Barrier Duration: 45 sec, Enemy Blows Blocked: 9, Damage: +25%
Damage -30% only for attacks that inflict damage at a certain ratio of the Max HP
Cooldown: 180 sec

Active Hero's Echo
Level Requirement 200
Master Level 1
Description [Master Level: 1]
Increases the Attack Power and Magic ATT of all nearby players.
Cooldown: 300 sec
Level 1 MP Cost: 30, Attack Power and Magic ATT: + 4%, Duration: 40 min

Active Royal Guard
Master Level 1
Description Soul Shield nullifies enemy attacks and counterattacks. Counterattacks are unaffected by attack ignore and attack reflection. The Invincibility effect and Attack Power increase buffs are not affected by the Buff Duration increase effect.
You can guard while using skills.
Level 1 MP Cost: 20, become invincible when attacked for 4 sec, nullifying attacks and counterattacking for a set time after use. Attack Power increases for 20 sec per counterattack.
If you guard successfully while in Attack Power Increase buff state, counterattack damage, attack range, and Attack Power increases gradually, but the time for guarding decreases gradually.
[1st Time]: Max Number of Enemies: 6, Damage: 305%, Number of Attacks: 4, Attack Power: +10.
[2nd Time]: Max Number of Enemies: 7, Damage: 370%, Number of Attacks: 5, Attack Power: +15.
[3rd Time]: Max Number of Enemies: 8, Damage: 470%, Number of Attacks: 6, Attack Power: +20.
Cooldown: 6 sec

Passive Final Attack
Master Level 20
Description Chance to deliver an additional hit after a direct attack. Must have a One-handed Sword equipped.
Required Skill: Sword Mastery Lv. 3
Level 20 required to learn Advanced Final Attack.
Level 1 [Final Attack Skill] Has a 2% chance to deal a final attack that deals 31% damage 3 time(s).
20 [Final Attack Skill] Has a 40% chance to deal a final attack that deals 50% damage 3 time(s).

Active Soul Link
Master Level 20
Description Connect your soul to nearby allies to unify and bolster your powers. Periodically enhances party members in the Soul Link's range when Soul Link is active. When Royal Guard's counterattack succeeds, party members in the Soul Link's range are protected.
Can be toggled On/Off.
Level 1 MP Cost per sec: 15
[Mihile]: Damage: +1% per party member in the same map. If you are not in a party, you will be considered to be in a 1-person party.
[Party Members]: When Mihile succeeds with Royal Guard, creates a protective shield that is 0% of each party member's Max HP for 0.5 sec for party members in the Soul Link's range.
Periodically for 8 sec, party members in the Soul Link's range receive a bonus to Attack Power and Magic ATT equal to 12% of the Attack Power bonus from Royal Guard. If Advanced Royal Guard is active, they will receive 1% of its Status Resistance and 11% of its DEF Bonus.
20 MP Cost per sec: 15
[Mihile]: Damage: +5% per party member in the same map. If you are not in a party, you will be considered to be in a 1-person party.
[Party Members]: When Mihile succeeds with Royal Guard, creates a protective shield that is 10% of each party member's Max HP for 10 sec for party members in the Soul Link's range.
Periodically for 8 sec, party members in the Soul Link's range receive a bonus to Attack Power and Magic ATT equal to 50% of the Attack Power bonus from Royal Guard. If Advanced Royal Guard is active, they will receive 20% of its Status Resistance and 30% of its DEF Bonus.

Passive Offensive Defense
Master Level 20
Description The power of the shield protecting the Empress makes enemies vulnerable to Mihile's Radiant Soul. Enemies hit with Royal Guard's counterattack receive a debuff. Using Radiant Soul skill to attack enemies with the debuff creates a light shockwave that does an additional attack.
The light shockwave is centered on the boss with the highest Max HP among those hit with the Radiant Soul skill. If there is no boss, then it's centered on the closest enemy among those hit.
Level 20 required to learn Advanced Offensive Defense.
Level 1 When Royal Guard's counterattack hits, give enemy Offensive Defense debuff for 20 sec
When Radiant Soul skill hits enemy with the debuff, a light shockwave is created centered on the enemy that was hit. The Offensive Defense debuff disappears when the enemy is hit by the light shockwave.
Light Shockwave - Max Enemies Hit: 6, Damage: 217%, Number of Attacks: 5
Cooldown: 12 sec
20 When Royal Guard's counterattack hits, give enemy Offensive Defense debuff for 20 sec
When Radiant Soul skill hits enemy with the debuff, a light shockwave is created centered on the enemy that was hit. The Offensive Defense debuff disappears when the enemy is hit by the light shockwave.
Light Shockwave - Max Enemies Hit: 6, Damage: 350%, Number of Attacks: 5
Cooldown: 12 sec

Active Erda Nova
Master Level 25
Description Collect Erda from within yourself and from the surrounding area, then detonate it around your enemies. The Erda of attacked enemies will become disrupted, which will bind their movements. Can deal damage to enemies even when they are under Attack Ignore. Also ignores Attack Reflection.
Level 1 HP Cost: 15% of Max HP, Damage: 156%, Max Enemies Hit: 10, Number of Attacks: 5, Bind Duration: 10 sec.
Bind Duration increases by up to 100% based on damage inflicted with Erda Nova.
Cooldown: 216 sec.

Active Erda Shower
Master Level 25
Description Fires a blast of compressed Erdas at nearby enemies.
Pressing the skill key with the down arrow key summons an Erda Fountain, an object filled with pure Erda.
With Action Customization enabled, you can summon Erda Fountain by pressing its skill key again, without the use of the arrow keys.
Right-click to toggle Action Customization ON/OFF

Active Decent Holy Fountain
Master Level 25
Description Summon a Holy Fountain that restores party members' HP. Even party members with the Undead status can use it. Approach the fountain and press the up arrow key to heal.
Can't be used on a map where another party member's Holy Fountain or Decent Holy Fountain already exists.
If the Decent Holy Fountain disappears before its duration ends, a Vestige of Divinity will remain. cCan't be used on a map where another party member's Holy Fountain, Decent Holy Fountain, or Vestige of Divinity already exists.
Not affected by effects which reset cooldowns, increase recovery skill potency, or increase summon duration. Cannot be summoned near a portal.
Level 1 HP Cost: 5% of max HP, Duration: 31 sec, restores 5% HP when used, able to use 5 times total.
If it disappears before duration is up, Vestige of Divinity is created in the remaining time.
Cooldown: 89 sec
[Passive Effect - All Stats: +1]
25 HP Cost: 5% of max HP, Duration: 55 sec, restores 30% HP when used, able to use 17 times total.
If it disappears before duration is up, Vestige of Divinity is created in the remaining time.

Active Phalanx Charge
Master Level 25
Description Summons brave Spearmen of the Cygnus Knights to charge enemies in a phalanx formation. The spearmen slow down upon touching an enemy. Press the skill key again to change their direction of movement. Unaffected by attack reflection and can be resisted by some monsters.
Level 1 MP Cost: 500, Damage: 468%, Number of Attacks: 41
Spearmen disappear when the number of attacks is reached, they move a certain distance, or after a certain duration. Activate the skill again to change their direction.

Description Infuses your weapon with a portion of your health, granting it a visible aura and temporarily empowering it. The aura wave is unaffected by attack reflection. Affected by effects which reduce cooldown.
Level 1 HP Cost: 10% of Max HP, Ignores 10% Enemy DEF for 82 sec, Final Damage: +1%.
Aura Wave (usable every 5 sec) - Using certain offensive skills will generate waves, inflicting 520% damage on up to 10 enemies, 6 times.
Weapon Aura Prepared: every 180 sec, Max Number Prepared: 2
25 HP Cost: 10% of Max HP, Ignores 15% Enemy DEF for 130 sec, Final Damage: +5%.
Aura Wave (usable every 5 sec) - Using certain offensive skills will generate waves, inflicting 1000% damage on up to 10 enemies, 6 times.
Weapon Aura Prepared: every 180 sec, Max Number Prepared: 2
30 HP Cost: 10% of Max HP, Ignores 16% Enemy DEF for 140 sec, Final Damage: +6%.
Aura Wave (usable every 5 sec) - Using certain offensive skills will generate waves, inflicting 1100% damage on up to 10 enemies, 6 times.
Weapon Aura Prepared: every 180 sec, Max Number Prepared: 2

Master Level 25

Damage increases +6% when hit, Max Stack: 3 times
Cooldown: 120 sec

Active Shield of Light
Master Level 25
Description Become a shield for your fellow party members. Temporarily blocks the damage and debilitating status conditions on party members inside the area, and increases your Final Damage.
Level 1 MP Cost: 1000, Duration: 41 sec, Final Damage: +21%
Damage Reduction (to you and party members inside shield): 68% (including Percentage HP attacks) for 25 sec, blocks debilitating status conditions
Upon successful blocking of the attack and status conditions, the shield has 3 layers, which can defend against 6, 6, and 11 attacks, respectively. Number of blocks decreases only once when both status condition and attack are applied at the same time.
Cooldown: 180 sec
25 MP Cost: 1000, Duration: 89 sec, Final Damage: +30%
Damage Reduction (to you and party members inside shield): 80% (including Percentage HP attacks) for 25 sec, blocks debilitating status conditions
Upon successful blocking of the attack and status conditions, the shield has 3 layers, which can defend against 9, 9, and 14 attacks, respectively. Number of blocks decreases only once when both status condition and attack are applied at the same time.
Cooldown: 180 sec
30 MP Cost: 1000, Duration: 99 sec, Final Damage: +33%
Damage Reduction (to you and party members inside shield): 83% (including Percentage HP attacks) for 25 sec, blocks debilitating status conditions
Upon successful blocking of the attack and status conditions, the shield has 3 layers, which can defend against 10, 10, and 15 attacks, respectively. Number of blocks decreases only once when both status condition and attack are applied at the same time.
Cooldown: 180 sec

Cooldown: 180 sec

Active Radiant Soul
Master Level 25
Description Draw on your soul power and imbue your sword with a radiant light. You can use Radiant Soul Slash with a regular attack while equipping Radiant Soul. Using Action Customization allows you to use Radiant Soul Slash with a regular attack or #Radiant Cross#. By reusing the skill, you can use Light Force Rei, which emits intense light, one time.
While the skill is in use, the Royal Guard's debuff is applied with max stacks. The afterimage of the sword is unaffected by attack reflection.
Action Customization Lock: Right-click
Level 1 MP Cost: 1200
Equip a Sword of Light for 35 sec., empowering your attacks. Final Damage: +5%, Critical Rate: +100%, and Ignore Defense: +100%. Increases the duration of Royal Guard to a total of 0.5 sec.
While active, the afterimage of the sword periodically falls upon up to 4 enemies, attacking 5 times for 468% damage.
Radiant Soul Slash: [Radiant Soul Skill] MP Cost: 100, Max Enemies Hit: 8, Damage: 598%, Number of Attacks: 12
Light Force Rei: [Radiant Soul Skill] Max Enemies Hit: 8, Damage: 982%, Number of Light Attacks: 15, Number of Light Attack Occurrences: 7.
When Radiant Soul Slash and Light Force Rei hits, 50% chance to Blind for 10 sec and decrease Accuracy by 30%
Cooldown: 180 sec.
25 MP Cost: 1200
Equip a Sword of Light for 35 sec., empowering your attacks. Final Damage: +9%, Critical Rate: +100%, and Ignore Defense: +100%. Increases the duration of Royal Guard to a total of 0.5 sec.
While active, the afterimage of the sword periodically falls upon up to 4 enemies, attacking 5 times for 900% damage.

Light Force Rei: [Radiant Soul Skill] Max Enemies Hit: 8, Damage: 1870%, Number of Light Attacks: 15, Number of Light Attack Occurrences: 7.
When Radiant Soul Slash and Light Force Rei hits, 50% chance to Blind for 10 sec and decrease Accuracy by 30%
Cooldown: 180 sec.

Active Sol Janus: Dawn
Master Level 30
Description Summon a Cyclic Ring that endlessly creates and destroys Sol Erda. The cycling Erda Flow attacks nearby enemies.
When a new ring is summoned, the Erda Flow of each ring is reduced. Cyclic rings can be summoned in midair but can't be summoned too close to or too far from an existing ring.
Cyclic Rings are unaffected by attack reflection.

Lv. 30: Normal Monster Damage: +30%
Level 1 HP Cost: 10% of Max HP
Ring Duration: 60 sec, Max Number of Rings: 1
Cyclic Ring - Max Enemies Hit: 10, Damage: 400%, Number of Attacks: 6

Master Level 30
Description Soul Shield nullifies enemy attacks and counterattacks the enemy. Counterattacks are unaffected by attack ignore and attack reflection. The Invincibility effect and Attack Power increase buffs are not affected by the Buff Duration increase effect.
Required Skill: Advanced Royal Guard Lv. 10
Level 1 MP Cost: 30, Become invincible when attacked for 4 sec, nullifying attacks and counterattacking for a set time after use. Attack Power increases for 20 sec per counterattack.
If you guard successfully while in Attack Power Increase buff state, counterattack damage, attack range, and Attack Power increases gradually, but the time for guarding decreases gradually.

Enhancements

Enhancements require the corresponding V Skill to be leveled to max and equipped. Final Damage bonuses from Enhancements increase linearly each level, with a jump at levels 10, 20, and 30.
